———————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————
                               SUPER MARIO RPG:
                           LEGEND OF THE SEVEN STARS
                                Text dumped by
                            TheRewster, a.k.a. Rew
                           Updated: January 19, 2015
———————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————

Note: This text dump is extracted from the North American version of the game, 
released May 13, 1996 for the Super Nintendo Entertainment System.

What follows is a cleaned-up presentation of all the text in the entire game--
not only dialogue but also menu text, item and monster lists, etc. I am heavily
indebted to the Lazy Shell editor on this project--kudos to the team behind 
that wondrous piece of software! One thing about this game is that there is a 
*lot* of duplicate text stored in the ROM, as well as a lot of empty slots for 
items marked by the game with the term "DUMMY." For completion's sake, all such
instances are included.

There is a "raw" version of this text dump--showing all the extra bits of 
control code in the text--available at Romhacking.net. (Just go to "Documents" 
and search for "mario rpg text dump," which should bring it up as one of the  
search results.) However, all such codes have been removed from this version to
give it a cleaner presentation.

The ordering of the text is fairly haphazard. After starting with the names of 
the five party numbers in one part of the ROM, the next part (and the vast 
majority of all the text) is the actual in-game dialogue--itself in just 
vaguely chronological order. The rest of the text, in the order in which they 
appear in the ROM (and thus in this document) are the monster attacks, battle 
dialogue, monster names, Psychopath messages, spell names, battle messages, 
spell descriptions, item descriptions, item names, miscellaneous menu text, and
world map location names.

For any questions, or if there are any errors, omissions, inconsistencies, or 
other issues, please email me at therewster1106@gmail.com--be sure to include 
"Mario RPG Text Dump" or something similar in the subject line so I know it's 
not spam.

 Eh hem...very well.
 “FP”s are consumed during
 battle when you use “Special”
 attacks. For example...

 A “Jump” attack uses 3 “FP”s.
 When you “Jump”, your “FP” will
 decrease by 3 each time. Run out,
 and you can't use these attacks!

 An item called a “Flower” raises
 your maximum “FP”s.
 Recover “FP”s with syrups,
 some mushrooms, and at inns.
———————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————————


 Eh hem...very well.
 “FP”s are consumed during
 battle when you use “Special”
 attacks. For example...

 A “Jump” attack uses 3 “FP”s.
 When you “Jump”, your “FP” will
 decrease by 3 each time. Run out,
 and you can't use these attacks!

 An item called a “Flower” raises
 your maximum “FP”s.
 Recover “FP”s with syrups,
 some mushrooms, and at inns.
